Local Communications II

Songjiang

District Head Approves Funds for Court Establishment: Yao, a court clerk from the High Court, was previously dispatched to Songjiang to prepare for the establishment of the county court. He once consulted with lawyers. Today (22nd), he summoned the district heads and various local organizations to a meeting. The establishment of the county court and the relocation and repair expenses of the Public Security Bureau would require a total of 5,000 yuan. In addition to the 1,000 yuan raised by lawyers, the district heads have resolved to temporarily allocate 2,000 yuan from the interest income of the municipal and rural public funds, while also raising funds to repay it. The remaining 2,000 yuan will be discussed and resolved by various organizations in a future meeting.

Provincial Girls' School Triumphant Return After Sports Victory: At this year's joint provincial school sports meet, Hu Ruisheng, Shen Ruizhi, Lu Xueqin, Xi Shaoye, Zhang Cuidai, Xu Zhiwan, and Tang Yajie, seven students from Songjiang Provincial Girls' High School, achieved victories in various sports programs, winning a total of 30 points. The school's overall score earned them first place. Hu Ruisheng also won first place in individual scores, with 39 points in the provincial public sports meet. Shen Ruizhi also won first place in the individual overall score, receiving more than 20 banners, silver cups, and other prizes. This morning, the athletes returned to Songjiang in triumph. The entire school lined up to welcome them, singing welcome songs along the way. The prizes were paraded around the city for a week, accompanied by military music.

Water and Land Police Disperse Gang of Bandits: Yesterday, the water police dispersed a gang of bandits attacking Zhu Jing. It is learned that the bandits numbered about seven or eight hundred, exceeding the number of water and land public security teams by almost double. The reasons for their defeat were firstly, Captain He Changlin, after the firearms of Zhang Hanbo's family security team were robbed in Maoqiao, remained on guard day and night; secondly, Inspector Zhang Yunfeng of the district headquarters led a shallow-water warship, and a patrol team composed of elite members drawn from various teams, arrived upon hearing the alarm, adding fresh troops to the battle. At the same time, the bandits' large red flag was hit by the warship's steel cannon and broke in two. With a shout, they retreated while fighting. The bandits considered the broken flag an ominous sign, so they fled. When the firing started, people in Zhu Jing and Feng Jing fled in panic. After the ceasefire in the afternoon, order gradually returned. Strict guard was maintained last night. Two dead bandits were intercepted on a bandit ship, and their heads were cut off and displayed in Zhu Jing Town as a warning. The public security team inspector of Jinshan County injured his ankle. There is no accurate information on the number of water police injured. However, it is known that Captain He personally went to Minhang today (22nd) to meet with District Head Chi to report the situation and request instructions on defense and suppression measures. The Songhu Garrison Headquarters, after receiving news of the bandit disturbance in Zhu Jing, immediately telegraphed the Songjiang County Government to investigate and report. County Magistrate Jin immediately sent personnel to secretly investigate the bandits' whereabouts. The headquarters also commissioned staff officer Zheng Qingtao to come to Songjiang for on-the-spot investigation. Currently, post-disaster prevention and maintenance are underway. The county public security team is guarding the No. 31 and No. 34 iron bridges to block the main road into Mao Lake. In addition to the above two iron bridges, Xin Zhen Fanbang, where the three counties of Jia, Qing, and Song meet, located north of Feng Jing and south of Qingpu, is also a gathering and dispersal place for the bandits. Patrol teams will also be dispatched there. It is reported that Taibao A Shu retreated in several directions yesterday, but at the same time, he also infiltrated in several directions. At 3:00 PM on the 17th, Zhang Hanbo's home in Maoqiao, in the western part of Jin County, was raided by a part of the bandits, who robbed a large number of rifles, boxes, cannons, steel wire vests, military knives, and self-defense team uniforms, and kidnapped a member of the security team, Qi Shushan. This group also joined the main force in retreating yesterday. The kidnapped member of the security team is still missing.

Suzhou

Rapist and Murderer Executed: Wang Zhangrong, a resident of Yonglong Town, Chongming County, had an affair with Mao Xu, the wife of his neighbor Mao Kuilang, in the 15th year of the Republic. Fearing that Mao Kuilang would find out, Wang sneaked into Mao's house on the 7th day of the eighth lunar month of that year. He found Mao lying on a table. Wang put a white cloth strip around Mao's neck and strangled him to death. Afterwards, Wang colluded with Mao Xu to hang the body on a beam, making it look like a suicide. Mao Kuilang's brother, Mao Jinfu, discovered the truth and reported it to the county government, which arrested Wang. After investigation and trial, Wang was sentenced to death. Wang refused to accept the verdict and appealed to the High Court for a retrial, which upheld the death sentence. Wang still refused to accept it and appealed to the Supreme Court. The third instance rejected the appeal and upheld the original verdict. After receiving the order, Chief Prosecutor Wang Simao of the High Court sent personnel to the No. 3 Branch Prison on Siqian Street at 9:00 AM yesterday (22nd) to bring out the prisoner Wang Zhangrong, verify his identity, and execute him by hanging according to the law.

Measures for Protecting and Rewarding Released Prisoners: Chief Judge Lin and Chief Prosecutor Wang of the Jiangsu High Court recently received an order from the Ministry of Justice and Administration, stating that the reform of prisoners should be emphasized during prison extraction. However, after their release, they often lack assistance and cannot make a living, leading to re-offending and imprisonment. Therefore, five articles of reward rules for the protection of released prisoners have been formulated and recorded as follows: (1) Those who handle the protection of released prisoners shall be rewarded in accordance with these rules. (2) Rewards are divided into the following two categories: (A) Those who have handled the matters in the preceding article for more than three years and have achieved outstanding results, or who have donated more than one thousand silver yuan, will be given a certificate of commendation. (B) Those who have handled the matters in the preceding article for more than five years and have achieved outstanding results, or who have donated more than five thousand silver yuan, will be given a plaque. (3) The rewards in each item of the preceding article shall be submitted by the local warden to the supervisory authority for review and referral to the Ministry of Justice and Administration for approval. (4) The written request submitted by the warden must separately record the following items: (A) Regarding those who handle affairs: (1) The age and origin of the person handling the affairs. (2) The process of handling the affairs and the future plans. (3) The number of years and achievements in handling the affairs. (B) Regarding those who donate silver yuan: (1) The age and origin of the donor. (2) The amount of silver donated. (5) The rewards in item A of the second article shall be executed by the Ministry of Justice and Administration, and the rewards in item B shall be submitted by the Ministry of Justice and Administration to the Executive Yuan for referral to the National Government for execution. After receiving the order, Chief Judge Lin and Chief Prosecutor Wang ordered the county magistrates, the new and old wardens, and the presidents of local courts to comply with and implement the order yesterday (22nd).

Request for Strict Investigation of Soil Transportation: Duan, the section chief of the Suzhou section of the Jinghu Railway, reported that recently, near the Tiger Hill area, when trains passed by Shiren Shima, opium was thrown out and picked up by armed local militias in accordance with pre-arranged plans. There were also many armed guard groups protecting the transport of opium, and armed personnel engaged in opium seizing, leading to occasional conflicts. Yesterday (22nd), he specially requested the police departments of both railways to send security teams to guard and arrest, and to strictly investigate the locomotives coming from both the Jing and Hu directions.

Reactionary Prisoners Riot in Detention Center: Xu Jiajin, Zhu Jichen, Chen Bojian, Zhu Shunde, and other reactionary prisoners detained in the Jiangsu No. 3 Prison Branch organized various departments in the prison and forcibly forced criminal prisoners to join the riot. Director Xia learned of this and attempted to persuade them at 1:00 PM on the day before yesterday (21st). Unexpectedly, the prisoners dragged Xia into the Jingzi prison cell, shouting slogans to overthrow the director, intending to tie him up. Fortunately, guards Du and Wan, along with the entire armed guard, arrived and rescued Xia. Director Xia telegraphed the Western District and dispatched police to the scene. The four prisoners, including Xu, were sent to Xiaoliuzhen to be shackled and imprisoned in the No. 3 Prison, and a report was submitted to the High Court for approval.

Wuxi

Choice of Section Chief for the Department of Civil Affairs: After the former Director of the Jiangsu Department of Civil Affairs, Pei Cheng, handed over his duties on the 20th, he hurriedly returned to his hometown that evening. Qian Sunqing, the section chief of the first section, also completed the handover of department affairs and returned to Wuxi first. The newly appointed Director Hu Pu'an, considering Qian's familiarity with politics, still requested Qian to continue serving as the section chief of the first section of the Department of Civil Affairs. He telegraphed yesterday to urge him. However, Qian, due to practical reasons, was unable to take on the role. He immediately telegraphed back to firmly decline and decided to go to the province on Monday to explain everything.

Resolution of Strike by Stone Industry Workers: Stone workshop workers in Wuxi went on strike on the 18th to demand wage increases from employers. However, they had not contacted the employers beforehand. After earnest mediation by the county chamber of commerce and representatives from both labor and management, it was decided to increase wages by four points per worker based on previous wages. Both parties reached an agreement, and work resumed as usual yesterday.

Municipal Committee Ordered to Abolish: The Wuxi Municipal Preparatory Office was established in the autumn of last year, with County Magistrate Sun Zuji concurrently serving as director. Initially, it was planned to abolish the county and establish a city, but due to the lack of legal basis, it was repeatedly delayed. Finally, it was planned to establish an ordinary city, but it still could not be realized due to various reasons. Before the former Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Miao Bin, stepped down, he instructed Director Sun to reorganize the municipal office into a municipal committee. After receiving the order, Director Sun proposed a municipal office meeting yesterday to resolve the matter by convening a meeting of municipal discussion committee members. However, news from the province stated that the municipal committee also lacked a basis and could not legally manage the city's municipal affairs. Therefore, there is talk of a clear order to abolish it. All matters to be handled should be transferred to the First District Office. Therefore, the issue of the survival or abolition of the Municipal Preparatory Office is a matter of great concern to the people of Wuxi.

Suspect Arrested in Tragic Murder Case: Yang Xianyi's home in Sibao Lane outside the North Gate of Wuxi County was suddenly attacked by six wandering bandits on the evening of the 17th of this month, who opened fire and killed Yang's eldest son, Quan Jin, and the cook, Wu Rensheng. It is now learned that the culprit in this case was arrested at around 6:00 PM yesterday by the victim Yang Xianyi, together with Xiao Tongsheng, the patrol chief of the second team of the Second Public Security Bureau, near the gate of the Qitai Inn on the road. The suspect, Liu Keli, was taken to the bureau for preliminary interrogation. Liu Keli claimed to be 23 years old and from Jiangxi, and denied any involvement in the murder. Yang Xianyi questioned him, and Yang firmly stated that this person was indeed the one who shot and killed his son on that day. He was immediately transferred to the county government for interrogation.

Fire Brigade Organization: Merged into Five Major Districts: There are more than 30 fire brigades inside and outside Wuxi County. Recently, at a county administrative meeting, someone proposed to merge the brigades into five major districts: east, south, west, north, and central. Each district would have a telephone and a bell tower for reporting fires. Yesterday, the county government, based on the resolution, sent letters to the Municipal Preparatory Office and the Fire Brigade Joint Association for review and implementation.

Bandit Uprising in Qigan District: On the 20th, more than 200 bandits rioted in the Erqian area of Qigan District, looting and destroying more than ten civilian homes. The provincial and county police teams immediately rushed to suppress them.

Opium Traffickers Rampant: Opium traffickers in Nantong County have recently been protected and are openly active. More than 5,000 taels of opium are transported into Yaogang Port every day. It is said that the sales area extends to Taizhou and Jingjiang in Jiangbei. Public opinion throughout the county is in uproar.

Judicial Funding Shortage: The Nantong County Court is currently hearing cases, but the county government has retained more than 10,400 yuan in judicial fees, which have not yet been transferred. President Dong has sent a letter to County Magistrate Chen stating that there are currently only more than 2,800 yuan available, a significant difference. He has specially requested the High Court to review and instruct.

County Magistrate Chen's Resignation Not Approved: County Magistrate Chen Buchan of Nantong has tendered his resignation to the provincial government due to difficult handling of affairs. He has been ordered to stay in his position. Chen is procuring firearms for the self-defense team in Shanghai and is scheduled to return to Nantong on the 23rd.

Court President Sworn into Office: The Nantong County Court has been officially established. President Dong Banggan and Chief Prosecutor Zhu Ronggui will be sworn into office on the 24th. Teachers' Meeting: Salary Collection Measures: The City District Teachers' Association held a meeting at the Public Lecture Hall due to the accumulated arrears of school funds for three months. (2) Convene a meeting of the Teachers' Association Executive Committee and representatives from each school (one person) after the contact. (3) Send letters to the County Party Affairs Rectification Committee, requesting assistance. (4) Appoint Sun Weimin and Wang Dehe to go with the school principals to the Department of Education to state their grievances and urge the speedy appointment of a director.

Easing Road Work Incidents: County Magistrate Chen Nanxuan investigated the circumstances of the incident at Huojiaqiao and has reported the details to the Construction Department. The price of land used for roads is set at 40 yuan per mu. Expenses for labor, food, damage to houses and graves, and removal of obstacles have all been reported to the department for instructions. The county government has issued a notice to the public, ordering the Construction Department to distribute labor evenly and urging them to resume work as soon as possible.

Homicide in Changtan Village: Shu, the wife of farmer Wang Shunlong in Shang Changtan Village outside the Ma Lane Gate of Danyang County, was slightly attractive. Because Wang was away on business, evil young men in the village often seduced her. A few days ago, Wang Pingzi's son suddenly led a group of people to cause trouble, intending to extort money. Shu was unable to cope and was beaten and injured, leading to her suicide by hanging. Her family has now reported the case to the county for investigation.

Communist Suspect Transferred to Suzhou: Zhu Xiaozhen, a communist suspect, has been under investigation by the county government since her capture in Shanghai. She has now been transferred to the county high court for trial.

Bandit Commander Executes Bandit Criminals: The Bandit Suppression Headquarters in Huzhou executed three bandit criminals, Jiang Ronggui, Li Guangyu, and Li Jinshan, who were transferred from Changxing one after another. After detailed interrogation by the headquarters, the bandits confessed their crimes without reservation. Yesterday afternoon at 5:00 PM, the three criminals were brought out, their identities verified, and they were tied up and executed by firing squad in front of the headquarters.

Zhangbang Village Satin Robbery: In Zhangbang Village, about ten li east of Changxing in Huzhou, Gao Jinshou's family was relatively well-off. At about 9:00 PM the day before yesterday, forty or fifty bandits, each carrying firearms, broke through the wall and entered, looting all clothing, bedding, food, and rice. Before leaving, they also robbed Gao's son-in-law, Zhou Yuxuan, of his satin.

Section Chief Injured After Jumping Over Wall: Since the robbery in Xincang, Pinghu County, martial law has been in effect for days, along with various rumors. It is said that County Magistrate Fang received a threatening letter from the bandits, demanding tens of thousands of yuan. For a time, the rumors spread, and the entire county was in panic, especially the government officials. The night before last, the Shen family in Hentangjie fired three firecrackers during a housewarming ceremony. The county government recognized the sound of cannons. County Magistrate Fang and a certain section chief imitated Xue and Liu's old trick. The section chief accidentally injured his leg and waist and was sent to the hospital for treatment. County Magistrate Fang immediately returned to the office. Yesterday, the county government posted a notice prohibiting the firing of firecrackers, and violators would be arrested.

Update on Electric Light Plant: The routes and poles of the former Pinghu Electric Light Company outside the Dananmen have now been purchased by Minghua Factory. All the poles in the city have been ordered by Minghua Factory to be dismantled one after another and will be completed soon. The new factory of Minghua Factory outside the Nanmen has already started construction, and new machinery will also be transported there. It is expected that the electricity will be turned on all night within the next month.

Forcible Relocation of Graves on Fushan Mountain: It has been decided to renovate Fushan Mountain into a park. Since the deadline for relocating the graves on the mountain has passed on February 15th and many have not yet been relocated, the County Construction Bureau has decided to hire workers to carry out the relocation on behalf of the owners.

Deadline for Reporting Land Cases: The deadline for reporting land cases in Shaoxing has been extended repeatedly and has not yet been concluded. Yesterday, the province issued a final deadline, no later than the 15th day of the fourth month, to complete all cases.

Land Survey Underway: The Zhejiang Provincial Land Bureau is carrying out a planned land survey for the purpose of land reorganization. The survey team has now progressed to Shaoxing and has begun surveying. The county magistrate has instructed all villages to cooperate and assist.

Xiaoshan

Wanted Satin Bandits Live in Xing: Wang Guorong, Wang Ruihuo, Wang Yinfa, Wang Binglin, and other satin bandits from Huangcunwu, Heshangdian, in the southern countryside of Xiaoshan, kidnapped a child in Fuyang. The Fuyang government learned of this and sent detectives to Xiaoshan to arrest them. The bandits fled upon hearing the news. The Fuyang County Government has sent a letter to the Xiaoshan County Government requesting that the houses of the bandits be sealed. Upon receiving the letter, the county government immediately ordered the Public Security Bureau to handle the matter and report back.

Construction of Silkworm Cooperative Houses Causes Disaster: The model silkworm cooperative in the eastern countryside of Xiaoshan contracted the construction of its houses to Weng Changji Construction Factory in Hangzhou. Since construction began a month ago, the project has been progressing smoothly. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 18th, fifteen or sixteen young pile drivers were working on an umbrella frame about 18 feet high when the frame, made of cedar pillars and pine boards, suddenly collapsed. All the young workers fell to the side of the trench, which contained huge pine piles and rocks. Those who fell suffered broken heads and feet. Four were slightly injured, and seven were seriously injured. Four of them had broken bones and ruptured abdomens, and their flesh was unrecognizable, causing concern for their lives.

Family of Three Dies Tragically from Plague: A plague has recently broken out in Wangjiazhuang, Yansili, in the western countryside of Xiaoshan. A farmer named Wang, his second daughter-in-law, was still weaving in the evening. At eight o'clock in the evening, she suddenly contracted the plague. By the time her aunt entered the room to check on her the next morning, she was unresponsive. When the blanket was lifted, she was already dead. Her family also had two young children who were soon infected. Doctors were urgently called for treatment, but before the medicine could be brewed and administered, they also died one after another.

Shangyu

Sons of Village Head and Deputy Village Head Kidnapped: At about 7:00 PM the day before yesterday, seven bandits in short attire suddenly arrived at the home of Village Head Chuan Guozhi in Huangnikeng Village in the southern countryside. Five of them stood guard outside, while two others, carrying guns, entered the house and, on the pretext of asking for information, kidnapped Guozhi's twelve-year-old only son. They then went to the home of Deputy Village Head Fu Chengpin and, using the same means, abducted his eleven-year-old young son. A letter was left at each victim's home, instructing Guozhi to bring 7,000 silver dollars and Chengpin to prepare 5,000 silver dollars, to be used as ransom within five days in Pingkeng.

First Executive Committee Meeting of the Education Association: Yesterday afternoon, the Second First Executive Committee Meeting of the County Education Association was held. Xia Chanchen, Song Zongjiao, Yao E, Qian Yaoer, Yao Ruikun, Chen Yousan, and Zhang Guoxiang attended. Xia Chanchen, Xu Youzhi, and Yao Ruikun were elected as standing committee members.

Scheduled Discussion of Bandit Suppression Measures: The Ningbo Four County Bandit Suppression Headquarters has recently issued orders to various military and police forces to carefully plan protection measures to ensure security in response to repeated robberies in the city. It is planned to convene officers and soldiers from the city and county Public Security Bureau, security team, detective team, and land defense team in the auditorium of the headquarters on the 24th of this month to discuss measures.

Japanese Students Travel Through Ningbo: Suzuki Takuro, President of the Shanghai Toa Dobun Shoin, led 91 Japanese students on the Xinningshao steamboat to Ningbo yesterday morning to visit various attractions in Ningbo. Hefei

Hefei-Liuan-Shouxian Bandit Suppression News: More than a thousand communist bandits are entrenched in the Mapu and Dushan areas of the western countryside of Liuan, causing shock in Liuan City. However, Wei Lihuang, the commander of the Eighth Army in Hefei, sent the First Training Regiment led by Li to Liuan. Wang Peishi, the county magistrate of Hefei, also went to Liuan to suppress the bandits on the border of Hefei and Liuan. The first and second security teams of the county were able to dispatch troops to Sujiabu to suppress the bandits. After days of fierce fighting, by the 14th, the communist bandits in Mapu and Dushan had been driven back. County Magistrate Wang is scheduled to return to Hefei on the 16th. Wang Shike, the county magistrate of Shouxian, also personally led the police battalion to suppress the bandits led by Quan Guangyi and others, who had been entrenched for a long time in the Maji and Sanjuesi areas on the border of Hefei, Liuan, and Shouxian since the 13th. Yesterday, he telegraphed the Hefei County Government to send troops to block and attack.

Police Chief Arrested: It is reported that Fu Chuanshuo, the police chief of Sanhe Town, has been accused by many citizens of the town at the Eighth Army Headquarters of dereliction of duty and protecting opium and gambling. After investigation, the allegations were found to be true. On the 16th, the army headquarters ordered the police chief to be brought to the headquarters for detention pending investigation.

Educational News

China Wins the International Football Championship

Defeats Scotland 2-0 Yesterday

First Championship in Seven Years

The spring sunshine is bright, the wind is gentle, and the weather is warm. It is the time for athletes to show their skills. Yesterday, the Shanghai Chinese team defeated Scotland 2-0 to win this year's Shanghai International Football Championship. At the Chinese baseball field, more than ten thousand Chinese and Western men and women cheered, and the sound shook the earth. The sound of firecrackers was like an electric storm, booming and magnificent. How glorious! The Shanghai International Football Championship, which had never been won before, was won by China for the first time. It is like tasting a rare delicacy. From now on, the magnificent International Cup will also be engraved with the words (China) and the great achievements of the decisive battle with Scotland, to be left as a permanent memento. It is truly a new era for Shanghai's football world.

Championships Won by Various Teams Over the Years

The Shanghai International Football Championship started in 1908. Except for the four years when it was suspended during the European War, it has been held every year without interruption. England has won the most times, followed by Scotland. Football is the birthplace of England, and their skills are outstanding, so it is appropriate that their record is the best. The championships of each year are listed below:

1908···09 England 1909···10 England

1910···11 England 1911···12 Ireland

1912···13 England 1913···14 England

1914···25 England 1915···19 Suspension of War

1919···20 England 1920···21 England

1921···22 England 1922···23 England

1923···24 England 1924···25 Scotland

1925···26 Scotland 1926···27 Scotland

1927···28 England 1928···29 Portugal

1929···30 China

Looking at the above, a total of 18 years of competition, England has won 12 championships, Scotland has won 3 times, and Ireland, Portugal, and China have each won once.

First Championship in Seven Years

Our country participated in the competition in 1923. Counting the years, it has a history of seven years. The first session had mediocre results, but since then it has had a deep determination for international competition. From then on, it has worked hard in training. In the second session (that is, in 1924-25), it was able to meet Scotland in the final. At that time, the magnificent and enthusiastic cheers of more than ten thousand spectators on the Chinese baseball field still hovered in our minds. However, in the end, China was unfortunately defeated 0-4. Although the championship was not won, it was an honor to be able to gain the final right as China had only recently joined. Later, in the 1927-28 session, China and England were able to meet again in the final. At that time, China's strength was very strong, and there was great hope for the championship. Unexpectedly, the Jinan University football team went to Nanyang, and strong players such as Feng Junyou, Chen Zhenhe, and Liang Guansong were unable to join, resulting in a great reduction in strength and a tragic defeat of 2-4. This year, for the third time, it gained the final right and was able to defeat the once powerful Scottish team 2-0 and win the championship. The efforts of several years have now established a remarkable achievement. How happy to have fulfilled our wishes!

The Chinese Team Had Confidence Early On

The participants in this competition include five countries: China, Jewish, Portugal, Scotland, and England. Among them, besides the Jewish team having relatively weaker strength, the remaining teams are evenly matched, each with hopes of winning the championship. In the preliminary round, the Jewish team lost to Scotland, and in the second round, China defeated England and Scotland defeated Portugal. Observing the situation of the two groups at that time, China's victory over England showed genuine skill, while Scotland's defeat of Portugal was due to luck. Therefore, for yesterday's final between China and Scotland, the Western newspapers already made a decisive statement, saying that China could assuredly win. The reporter also held the same view. The fierce battle unfolded as expected, with a score of 2-0. It seemed quite laborious, but observing the competitive situation, China had many offensive opportunities. However, due to bad luck, they missed excellent chances no fewer than seven or eight times. Otherwise, the number of goals scored would have been far more than this.

Goals Scored All in the Second Half

The match began at 3:00 PM. In the first half, China attacked with the wind, creating a very strong momentum. However, the forwards appeared somewhat disorganized and lacked good cooperation, resulting in their inability to capitalize on opportunities. The audience was very anxious, believing that if they couldn't win in the first half, they would face difficulties and disadvantages fighting against the wind in the second half. Unexpectedly, in the second half, the forwards' connection suddenly improved, and their short passing skills were excellent. Chen Yutian's right wing became even more courageous, and his two crosses were hit by Dai Linjing, allowing China to win the championship. Both inside and outside players were able to coordinate seamlessly, resulting in ample strength, making it difficult for the opponent to develop their game. Center-back Sun Sijing and goalkeeper Zhou Xianyan both performed outstandingly. Among the forwards, Chen Yutian was the best, being small and agile, running quickly. The tall and strong foreigners were unable to catch him. Chen's corner kicks were almost always accurate, making him a rare talent. It is a pity that his passing footwork was too slow, which was his only flaw.

Scotland Lacked Coordination

As for the Scottish side, defender [Big Guy] Turner was the best, while the rest were average. The forwards lacked coordination. Even when the ball reached China's goal, they lacked mutual support, thus missing scoring opportunities. In addition, their kicking accuracy was poor, making it difficult to execute plays. There was a disconnect between the forwards and the midfielders. When the forwards attacked, the midfielders often didn't move forward to support them. When the ball was returned, there were often no opportunities to continue the attack. This was a major problem. They didn't show much energy throughout the first half. After conceding a goal in the second half, their momentum slightly improved, and their several incursions caused considerable panic for China. Ultimately, the Scottish team's strength was weak, making their efforts futile. The lineups of the two teams are as follows:

China Immediately Gained the Upper Hand After Kickoff

After the coin toss, the Scottish team got the right to kick off. Due to fighting against the wind, their strength was reduced. China seized the opportunity to take advantage. Li Huitang used a high ball to pass to Wang Yongjie, who sent it to the front of the goal. Dai Linjing and Chen Yutian went up together. At that time, the opponent's goal was relatively open, and they could have calmly advanced. Unexpectedly, Dai's header missed. A golden opportunity was lost. However, China's momentum did not weaken. Chen Yutian's passes were very effective. The ball fell along the crossbar of the Scottish goal. The Scottish goalkeeper jumped up and pushed it to the rear. Yutian continued to kick a corner, and although the cross was good, it didn't yield any results.

National Games Football Championship Final: Photo of the Chinese and Scottish Teams (Photographed by Wang Kai)

China Repeatedly Missed Opportunities

Sun Sijing sat in the center-back position, responding effectively. He intercepted the opponent's counter-attacks from the rear three times in a row and attacked the Scottish goal, but they were all saved. Although China repeatedly missed opportunities, they did not lose heart. On the contrary, they appeared spirited, with momentum like a tide. The ball often penetrated from the right side, thanks to the efforts of right-winger Chen Yutian. Once, Li Huitang got the ball 20 yards in front of the opponent's goal. He stopped, paused, and kicked forcefully towards the goal. The audience thought it would be a sure goal, and the opponent's fortress could be taken down at any moment. Unexpectedly, it hit the foot of an enemy player and bounced back. Opportunities were repeatedly missed, causing frustration.

The First Half Passed Uneventfully

Scotland weathered the storms repeatedly, doing their best to resist, and finally repelled the enemy. Then, they launched a counter-attack. Center-back Morrow kicked a high ball to the front of the Chinese goal. Chinese inner-back Jiang Shan fell, and the opponent's left-inner forward rushed forward to seize the ball. After a few steps, he was just about to shoot. Jiang saw the danger and turned back to chase. The ball was blocked. Shortly after, the Scottish right-winger kicked a corner kick. The landing point was very good. After a long melee, finally 克萊忽 got the ball five or six yards from the right corner of the goal and shot towards the goal, hitting Zhou Xianyan squarely. Zhou was quick-eyed and quick-handed, catching it immediately, dodging the enemy, and sending it forward with a kick, turning danger into safety. Afterwards, they galloped back and forth, each achieving something. The first half passed peacefully.

China Opened the Scoring in the Second Half

After a brief lemon break, they switched directions and continued to play. Although China was facing the wind, their strength appeared to increase. Li Huitang passed the ball to the right, and Chen Yutian dribbled the ball along the sideline, passing it to the Scottish goal. The ball skimmed the goal to the left. Wang Yongjie returned to the front of the goal. Just as the ball was about to enter the goal, Dai Linjing rushed forward and added a kick. The ball entered the goal, and cheers erupted instantly, shaking the sky. The sound of firecrackers was also continuous. The enthusiastic scene was beyond description.

Scotland Tried Hard to Counter-Attack

After conceding a goal, Scotland did not lose heart. On the contrary, they showed renewed courage, like 中瑪琲, trying hard to counter-attack, with a murderous aura. As a result, danger arose in front of the Chinese goal. They were surrounded on all sides, with no way out. High and Sinclair施劲 shot, and Zhou Xianyan almost became the target of all arrows. Fortunately, the inner-backs were heavily guarded, and Zhou Xianyan defended effectively, preventing any losses. However, China had already been frightened.

The Second Goal Was Kicked in by Dai

Amidst the chaos, Li Huitang received the ball kicked out by the Scottish right-winger and led the attack, sending the ball far to the right. Chen Yutian tracked and intercepted the ball, rushing past a barrier. He dribbled the ball at full speed, advancing heroically, straight into no man's land. At the same time, the audience applauded and cheered continuously. Yutian became even more inspired, rushing to the edge of the goal and passing it towards the front of the goal. Unexpectedly, no one was there to receive it, ruining all his efforts. But as one wave went, another came. The Scottish goal was surrounded again. The forwards used close-quarters combat, making it difficult for the enemy to figure them out. Dai Linjing kicked it suddenly, and the ball went into the net. China won by two goals. As a result, China's momentum became even stronger, and the shouts shook the sky. Li Huitang missed two opportunities, and Chen Jiaqiu also had bad luck, failing to score, which was regrettable.

Zhou Xianyan Saved the Ball with Quick Wit

Having conceded two goals, Scotland was unwilling to accept defeat and continued their efforts, intending to retaliate. Later, they kicked a free kick 30 to 40 yards from the Chinese goal. The ball was fast and powerful, landing right in front of the goal. Zhou Xianyan caught it but fumbled. Jiang Shan added a kick to get rid of danger. Unexpectedly, the Scottish right midfielder got it and returned it to the Chinese goal. The Scottish army rushed up. Zhou Xianyan was wrestled to the ground by the enemy, struggling to break free. Zhou had no choice. In desperation, he quickly threw the ball out of bounds, thus preventing further danger. Afterwards, China attacked again. Li Huitang shot forcefully at the goal, neither too high nor too low, with extreme power. The Scottish goalkeeper pushed it to the rear, showing his skills. The whole stadium praised him. As a result of the fierce battle, China won 2-0.

The Crowd Cheered When China Received the Award

After the match ended, the award was presented in the field. The chairman of the Western Football Association, Grishaw, gave a speech, saying that in this Shanghai International Football Competition, the Chinese team won the championship with their true skills, which was admirable. After Grishaw, he presented the silver cup to the Chinese team captain, Li Huitang. They cheered each other and dispersed.

Pittsburgh But Instructed to Heal Tournament Chinese Victory

▲Forty-seven to forty

▲Our country's technology is extraordinary

▲Rescheduled for next Wednesday and Saturday

The [healing] tournament between the Chinese basketball team and Pittsburgh adopted a best-of-three system. Last night, the first game between the two teams, following the International Women's Basketball, resulted in the Chinese team winning 47-40. The referees were Zhang Guoxun and Smith. The remaining two games are scheduled for next Wednesday and Saturday.

(1) Sea Monster Has Head but No Tail

Pittsburgh is known as the sea hegemon, nicknamed the "Sea Monster," and foreigners call them "Pirates." Their fierceness is evident. They came from the Philippines this time with great fanfare, sending a letter of challenge to avenge America. However, last night, when they faced China, they didn't show much brilliance. They beat the Chinese team by one point in the first half, but weakened in the second half. However, the Chinese team must still be cautious.

(2) Lu Zhong'en Still a Pillar

The Chinese team's lineup was slightly different from when they played against the United States. He Tongwei and Wei Haiqing were in the center forward position, Huang Yunli and Liang Guoquan were on the left and right, and Lu Li was the back. Last night's battle didn't seem as wonderful as when they won the International Championship. However, Chen Zhongen's command was smooth, and he was calm in the face of battle, with orderly tactics, making him the natural pillar of the entire team. Li Baojun's steadiness was universally praised, and Huang and Liang each had their own strengths.

(3) Pittsburgh's Ephemeral Brilliance

When the two armies made contact, Huang Yunli opened the scoring first, and Liang Guoquan followed with four, gaining the upper hand first and boosting morale. However, the Pittsburgh team quickly caught up, taking the lead with 8-7. After that, it was difficult to tell who would win. The two teams were separated by two points. The situation was tense, and the audience opened their eyes and stuck out their tongues, waiting for the outcome. In the morning, the Pittsburgh team actually won with 17-16, beating China by one point. However, this was just a brief flash of brilliance from the Pittsburgh team.

(4) The Chinese Team Sailed Smoothly

The lemon fight continued, with the score remaining close, with a difference of only one or two points. However, the Chinese team suddenly soared. Thanks to the joint efforts of Huang and Liang and Li Baojun's successful long-range shot, they were ahead of the Pittsburgh team with a score of 31-23. Perhaps the Pittsburgh team was unlucky. Center Huaer injured his foot and continued to fight with pain, but his strength was not diminished. Finally, he had to withdraw. Then, defender Parker was sent off for four fouls. The Chinese team had a smooth sailing, winning with 47-40.

Results of the International Women's Basketball Game Yesterday

▲England Wins America 34-32

▲The Federation Wins China 29-15

The International Women's Basketball competition was held at the Chinese Basketball Hall yesterday with two groups starting at 6:00 PM (1) England defeated America 24-32 (2) The Federation defeated China 29-15.

▲England wins America. The strength of the American team was unexpectedly defeated by the English team. The situation of the two teams was average. The American team's defeat can be said to be due to bad luck, with dozens of shots failing to go in. The English team's back used an excellent arc, causing the ball to fall in front of the basket. Harrison picked it up and put it in with one hand. England had a smooth run, resulting in a score of 34-32. The referee was Smith.

▲The Federation wins China. China's inability to defeat the Federation was expected. However, the situation in the first half showed that it was not entirely hopeless to defeat the Federation. The forwards Xi Jun, Chen Xinyuan, and Shao Jinying each had good skills, but their lack of coordination was a problem. The backs were weak. The loss was too late, making it impossible to resist Jie Hansen and Ciena's sharpness. In the first half, China won 11-9. The result was 29-15, with the Federation winning. The referee was Smith.

During the 1500-meter event, Dalian YMCA athlete Ma Degang, after running only 45 meters, was accidentally stepped on the side of his right foot by Northeast University athlete Pang Shirong with spiked shoes, resulting in a total of five wounds, approximately two fen deep, the longest about one cun in length, with blood flowing profusely. Despite the injury, Ma continued to run, but was unable to continue at 1300 meters and withdrew from the race. When everyone reached the finish line, they inquired about the cause. Ma then threw down his spiked shoe and said, "Everyone, please look." Only then did the crowd realize he was injured. He was treated at the Red Cross Hospital, where it was stated that the injury was not severe and he would recover in about two weeks. To emphasize the importance of athletic performance, the judges allowed him to be recorded as a 1500-meter athlete. (Huanhua)

News Highlights

Municipal Education Bureau Holds Meeting with Private Middle School Principals

The Shanghai Special Municipality Education Bureau convened its first meeting with principals of private secondary schools in the city on the afternoon of yesterday at 1:00 PM in the Education Bureau's conference room. Representatives from 32 schools, including Pudong Middle School, the affiliated middle schools of Datong, Hujiang, and Fudan Universities, Southern Middle School, Qingxin Girls' and Boys' Middle School, Zhonghua Middle School, Shibei Middle School, Southeast Women's Physical Education School, Bowen Girls' Middle School, and Zhonghua Patriotic Girls' School, attended. From the Education Bureau, Director Chen, Secretary Ni, Zhou Shang, and Zhang Tianen were present. Director Chen presided, Zhang Yanggao recorded the minutes, and proper etiquette was observed.

▲Chairman's Report: Today's meeting with private middle school principals is limited to those that are registered. This is the first such meeting in the city, and I will now outline the objectives of convening this meeting, which are roughly fourfold: (1) [The Education Bureau's Attitude Towards Municipal and Private Schools]: The Education Bureau values private schools as much as municipal schools. Running a private school is not just about providing education and operating a school; it has a public purpose. Investing in a private school without a public purpose is unsustainable and can even lead to rogue schools. Therefore, from a public perspective, the Education Bureau values private schools even more than municipal schools. For the generally good private schools in the city, we will support and supervise them to encourage their progress. Otherwise, we will seek ways to rectify them. If a private school has other purposes, it will be unable to improve the effectiveness of teaching. All the schools present today are excellent, and we hope they will help the Bureau develop education in the city. (2) [Importance of Middle Schools]: Shanghai has over a hundred private middle schools, most of which are registered. Many of the unregistered ones have also reported to the Bureau. The Bureau will establish a system to encourage those not yet registered to do so and hopes that all private middle schools will unite for mutual benefit. Those who obstruct this will be dealt with. It should also be noted that, given the current financial difficulties that prevent the implementation of compulsory education, we are somewhat lenient towards private elementary schools. However, this is not the case for middle schools. It seems that Chinese secondary education last month tended to be dual-track. Middle schools must cultivate both vocational skills and academic abilities for further education. Therefore, the status and nature of middle schools are very high. In today's China, the status of universities is not as important as that of middle schools. Given the current poverty and depleted resources, if we want to stabilize the foundation of the country, we must rely on a large number of middle-level talents. It is only with excellent middle schools that we can have excellent middle-level talents. This is why we are slightly lenient towards elementary schools but strict towards middle schools. In the past, private schools each operated independently, and the administrative authorities paid no attention to them, which was a big mistake. If the education administrative authorities only focus on the schools they directly control and ignore private schools, it will undoubtedly hinder the progress of education. (3) [Remedies for Middle Schools]: The current level of middle school students is lower than before. Middle school graduates cannot cope with all situations in society, especially in Shanghai. This should be blamed on the universities. Nowadays, so-called universities do not consider qualifications when admitting students, resulting in students who are ambitious but impractical. Therefore, those who are not strict in training in middle school will produce many superficial and unrealistic university students. Because universities are not strict in their admissions, middle schools have to accommodate them, resulting in a decline in standards. This phenomenon is regrettable. To remedy this, (a) we have already implemented the crackdown on substandard universities, and (b) the Bureau has requested the Ministry of Education to abolish university preparatory courses, which has been approved. The significance of this is that universities cannot indiscriminately recruit lower-level students through preparatory courses. At the same time, the difficulties of secondary schools can be slightly reduced. Because junior or senior high school students cannot easily enter university preparatory courses, universities have been allowing secondary school students in training to transfer to universities, which has resulted in unaccomplished academics and damaged character, which is extremely harmful. Therefore, abolishing university preparatory courses is a way to promote middle schools. In addition, the ease of transferring schools means that students do not have the opportunity for long-term training and cultivation. In my personal opinion, students who are good at transferring are not good students with excellent grades. We should find ways to remedy this, but we must first have sufficient preparation and a comprehensive plan. This is also a key objective of today's meeting. (4) [Testing Curriculum Standards]: Previously, different schools in different regions had different curricula, and teaching could not be improved. It was not until last year that the Ministry of Education issued regulations on curriculum standards. However, due to the need for universality, they cannot be suitable for all places. But with this standard, we can have something to follow. Now, the Bureau has drafted trial middle school curriculum standards according to needs and distributed them to schools for testing. In the future, each school will report the results of the tests to the Bureau, so that we can present them to the Ministry of Education as a basis for revision. The Education Bureau hopes that today's meeting will become a channel of communication between teaching and administrative agencies, so as to solve the difficulties of both sides. In addition, there are two other things: (1) The Education Bureau is now trying to support the development of private middle schools and does not intend to take them over after they have developed. This should be stated responsibly because it is our duty to promote the development of private schools. (2) The names of private schools should be unified. Many schools are called "Gongxue," "College," or "Elementary and Secondary School," which makes it difficult to understand their nature. They should be renamed "High School," "Junior High School," or "Middle School." If there is an elementary school, it should be called "Affiliated Elementary School." The four points I had to report are now complete. I will now ask the head of the relevant department to report. I will leave beforehand. Secretary Ni, who is also the department head, will chair the report later.

▲Principals' Reports: Each principal presented the difficulties of their respective schools in detail. The chairman responded to each item one by one.

▲Discussion: (1) Discussed and approved the standard for student tuition fees; (2) Discussed and approved the standard for student boarding fees; (3) Discussed and approved the standard for various miscellaneous fees. It was decided that the Education Bureau would collect forms from each school for statistical analysis before making a decision; (4) Discussed methods for schools to recruit transfer students. It was decided that schools should not recruit students into the third year of junior high school or the third year of high school. Other grades may be recruited, but they must obtain a transfer certificate or transcript and pass a transfer examination. For students with excellent academic performance who use a credit system, increase the credits for the next semester. For those who use a semester system, the ability grouping system can be used to develop their abilities; (5) Discussed the establishment of a public science laboratory for private secondary schools in Shanghai Special Municipality. It was decided that each private school would automatically organize and then the Bureau would provide support; (6) Discussed whether extracurricular activities should be given credit. It was decided that each school could give credit for extracurricular activities, and the results must be reported to the Bureau; (7) Discussed the establishment of a circulating library for private secondary schools in Shanghai Special Municipality. It was decided that the Bureau would try to request funds from the municipal government to establish it, and each private school would participate together; (8) Discussed urging the British and French Concession authorities to ban prostitution.

It was decided that the Bureau would send a letter to the municipal party headquarters and the Chinese Education Office of the Concession to request the municipal government to stop it and to pay more attention to training in schools. The meeting adjourned at half-past five.

Private Preparatory School for Studying in France

▲Failed to Comply with Regulations and Obtain Approval for Establishment

▲Municipal Education Bureau Prohibits Enrollment According to Law

The Municipal Education Bureau sent a letter to various newspapers yesterday, stating: "To whom it may concern: It has been discovered that someone has newly established a private preparatory school for studying in France within the campus of the East Asia University, which was ordered to be closed on Avenue Joffre. Without first complying with the regulations for private schools and obtaining approval for its establishment, it has immediately begun operations. In accordance with the decree issued by the Ministry in January of this year, which stipulates that secondary schools and higher established after February 1st of this year that have not been approved are prohibited from enrolling students, the aforementioned preparatory school is hereby prohibited from enrolling students. We are writing to inform your newspaper that all enrollment advertisements and school news from the aforementioned preparatory school should not be published. We would be grateful for your cooperation. Sincerely."

Taxpaying Chinese Association Yesterday

Elected Municipal Representatives

▲Yu Qiaqing and 27 Others

The highest authority of the Shanghai Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association is the Representatives' Assembly. Representatives are elected annually, with a total of 81 members, elected in three parts according to regulations: 27 members elected by the public, 27 members elected by mutual election among commercial groups, and 27 members elected by mutual election among hometown associations. This year is the ninth election. The 27 members elected by the public were voted on the day before yesterday at the Bankers' Association. The ballots were counted at 10:00 AM yesterday. Representatives from the municipal government Qi Xuan, from the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs Ye Hongji, Chinese committee members from the Public Works Department Lin Kanghou and Qian Longzhang, chairman of the Taxpaying Association Wang Xiaolai, Xu Jilong, standing committee members Lu Feiboong and Wu Yunzhai, executive committee members Zhang Yichen, Hu Fengxiang, Lu Wenzhong, Yu Mingxun, Yan Eersheng, representatives from the Chamber of Commerce Chen Songyuan, representatives from the Navigation Guild Cen Erjun, and reporters from various groups and newspapers were present. Chairman Wang Xiaolai and master of ceremonies Tao Leqin read the will of Sun Yat-sen and performed the ceremony. Chen Songyuan, Lu Wenzhong, Lin Kanghou, Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yichen, Zheng Yongyu, and Xu Yunhui were appointed as ballot counters, while Zhou Fuzhang, Yan Eersheng, Hua Ziming, Luo Cuisheng, Pei Yunqing, Zheng Baoyuan, and Zou Quan were appointed as vote readers. Representatives from the municipal government and the Shanghai office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs supervised the opening of the ballot box and counted the ballots. There were a total of 845 ballots, with 6 invalid ballots, leaving 839 valid ballots. The ballot readers and the staff of the association jointly read and counted the ballots until 4:00 PM. The chairman then announced the names of the elected candidates and the number of votes they received. After the public election was completed, the association will soon hold mutual elections for representatives from commercial groups and hometown associations. Once all 81 representatives have been selected, the Representatives' Assembly will be convened in accordance with regulations to formally elect Chinese directors and committee members of the Public Works Department and mutually elect 27 executive committee members to handle association affairs. The names of the 27 representatives elected by the public and the number of votes they received are listed below: (1) Yu Qiaqing, 390 votes; (2) Yuan Ludeng, 233 votes; (3) Fang Jiaobo, 207 votes; (4) Zhang Yichen, 183 votes; (5) Qin Runqing, 176 votes; (6) Qian Longzhang, 173 votes; (7) Hu Fengxiang, 167 votes; (8) Wang Xiaolai, 165 votes; (9) Bei Songsun, 148 votes; (10) Song Hanzhang, 133 votes; (11) Lin Kanghou, 118 votes; (12) Wu Zhihao, 112 votes; (13) Jiang Yiping, 110 votes; (14) Xie Zhongfu, 110 votes; (15) Zou Quan, 100 votes; (16) Sun Qiuping, 99 votes; (17) Chen Tianyin, 98 votes; (18) Zou Xiqing, 96 votes; (19) He Shaogeng, 96 votes; (20) Zhang Rulin, 92 votes; (21) Zhao Jinqing, 91 votes; (22) Shi Liangcai, 91 votes; (23) Zhang Yichen, 90 votes; (24) Chen Tingrui, 89 votes; (25) Yu Zhongxian, 87 votes; (26) Wang Rutang, 85 votes; (27) Huang Chuqiu, 83 votes (Note: Huang Chuqiu and Jin Runxiang had the same number of votes, and a drawing was held to determine the winner).

Ministry Approves Expansion of Jianghai Customs Area

The Ministry of Finance has approved the Shanghai Municipal Government's request to expand the Jianghai Customs area, extending upstream to Zhangjiatang Port and downstream to Wusong. It has instructed the Customs Administration to direct the Inspector General of Customs to conduct a thorough survey to determine whether this is appropriate for regulation. The report received stated that after investigation by the Jianghai Customs Commissioner, it was determined that the expansion was necessary to accommodate the development of Shanghai and was feasible. It also included detailed maps showing the boundaries of the extension for review. The Ministry has approved the request and has issued separate instructions for implementation.

No Progress in Discussions on Improving Concession Telephone Issues

The North China Daily News reported that the telephone issue in the concession is complex, with conflicting opinions, and may not be resolved in the short term. The current problem stems from the outdated equipment and insufficient funding of the China and Foreign Telephone Company, which has led to widespread criticism from the public. The Public Works Department began to take action several months ago but initially seemed to only negotiate directly with the company. Later, it established an advisory committee to discuss the matter and consider the bids from three companies: International Telephone & Telegraph Corporation, Ericsson Company, and Cables and Wireless. As a result, the terms of the franchise for the municipal authorities of the two concessions became a problem. Of the three bids, two companies' financial and business plans were largely based on the existing franchise rights of the China and Foreign Telephone Company, while the third company attached a proposal to revise the franchise. For the past two months, the Public Works Department and the Conseil d'Administration have been consulting back and forth but have been unable to agree on a common policy. Matters such as the new company's dividend rate (8% or 1%), the franchise term (10, 20, or 40 years), the future telephone rates, and the revision of the term have all become points of contention between the two parties. The meeting last Monday also made no progress. The Conseil d'Administration seems to be motivated by the Public Works Department's mismanagement of business, and therefore did not agree to the Public Works Department's latest proposal. There are rumors that the French Concession intends to form its own telephone company, but the authorities are currently still in the process of deliberate consultation. Telephone users, shareholders, the advisory committee, and bidding companies are becoming impatient. The prolonged delay means that the telephone company will be unable to expand, the work of the advisory committee will be in vain, and the time and money spent by the representatives of the bidding companies will be for naught.

Ministry Order on Preserving Old Archives

The Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs received an order from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs stating: "To Comply with Instructions: An order from the Executive Yuan states: An official communication from the Ministry of Education states that the National Peking Research Institute stated in a letter that the old archives of various provinces, counties, and cities are of great importance as historical materials. If they are not specially preserved, they may be destroyed over time. Please submit a request to the Executive Yuan and then to the National Government, ordering all provincial, county, and city agencies to properly preserve their old archives or hand them over to academic institutions for preservation and organization, and not to arbitrarily destroy them. The Ministry notes that the archives of various provinces, counties, and cities are of great importance to regulations, documents, and culture. All materials that can be used for historical research should be cataloged and carefully preserved. The request of the Research Institute is well-founded. It is appropriate to copy the original letter and submit it to the Executive Yuan and then to the National Government, ordering all national, provincial, county, and city agencies to comply with the procedures. The Executive Yuan then submitted the proposal to the National Government, and the 66th State Council meeting resolved to proceed with the matter. The Council has issued an order to comply. This order is hereby issued to the Ministry to comply and to instruct all its subordinate units to comply. This order." In addition to the report and order, this order is hereby issued to comply.

Drug Industry Dispute Unresolved After Mediation the Day Before Yesterday

▲Rescheduled for Mediation Next Monday

Regarding the labor-management dispute in the pharmaceutical industry, the Bureau of Social Affairs scheduled a mediation meeting the day before yesterday. Six representatives from the labor side and five from the management side attended. The negotiation began at 2 PM, chaired by Mr. Guo Yongxi from the Bureau. Negotiations continued until 6 PM, but no consensus was reached. Both parties then had dinner at the Bureau and resumed discussions, extending until 10 PM, still without resolution. The points of contention, it is said, are:

Page 14

The management insisted on absolute obedience to the city government's approval, giving priority to re-employment. The labor side insisted on implementing full placement as mandated by the Party. Chairman Guo then offered his opinion, stating that the Bureau had already formulated a plan for this mediation. The management should first re-employ the pharmaceutical workers registered with the Bureau, and the labor side should not make excessive demands. However, both parties expressed dissatisfaction with this plan. As the clock struck ten, Chairman Guo announced the adjournment and scheduled another mediation for next Monday.

Yesterday afternoon, the labor side revisited the City Party Headquarters to petition, resulting in a highly satisfactory outcome. It is generally believed that after the mediation on Monday, there should be no further issues.

Kiwa Cotton Mill Labor Strike Resolved

The labor strike at the Japanese-owned Kiwa Cotton Mill has been resolved after the Bureau of Social Affairs assigned personnel to convene labor and management representatives for mediation over several days, together with representatives from the City Party Headquarters and the Public Security Bureau. It is reported that a resolution was reached the night before last (the 21st) at 8:30 PM, stipulating four measures for resumption of work and fifteen agreed-upon conditions. Both parties were satisfied. Yesterday afternoon (the 22nd), all workers at the mill resumed work. The full text of the agreed-upon conditions is recorded below:

▲Decision by the Shanghai Special Municipality Labor-Management Mediation Committee　Disputing Parties: All Workers of Kiwa Cotton Mill (Labor Side). Kiwa Cotton Mill (Management Side). Regarding the dispute over the terms of employment, which the parties in question had disagreements about, this committee convened a mediation and obtained the consent of both parties. The following resolution is hereby made: Main Text All workers of Kiwa Cotton Mill and Kiwa Cotton Mill have agreed to fifteen terms of employment conditions on March 21, 1920 (Republic of China), which shall be regarded as a labor contract between the parties in dispute. (Full text of the conditions is attached below.) Reasons: The aforementioned conditions have been agreed upon and signed by both parties. According to the provisions of Article 3, Paragraph 2 of the Labor Dispute Resolution Law, they should be regarded as a labor contract between the parties in dispute. Terms of Employment Conditions Agreed Upon by All Workers of Kiwa Cotton Mill and Kiwa Cotton Mill: Article 1: Wage increases for workers shall be handled in accordance with the mill's previously established rules. Article 2: A rice subsidy of one yuan per month. Workers on shifts A and B will have five cents deducted for each day of work stoppage, and long-day workers will have six cents deducted. Article 3: Workers who have worked in the mill for a full year without being dismissed by the mill due to misconduct will receive a bonus of half a month's wages. This principle applies to other similar situations. Article 4: All workers who were laid off this time will be reinstated as before. Article 5: Female workers are not allowed to be transferred out under any circumstances. Article 6: Senior staff and foremen will be provided with a separate rest room by the mill. Article 7: Long-day workers will be assigned to work with all workers every two weeks. Article 8: The first day the mill reopens after the New Year, double wages will be paid. Tea money will be paid on the second, third, and fourth days, except for those who receive special bonuses. Article 9: Senior staff and foremen will use black blotting paper. Article 10: Accumulated wages shall not be confiscated, except in cases of workers absconding or theft. Article 11: The water supply in the workshop must be adequate. Article 12: The lights in the summer period must be bright enough. Article 13: Boiling water must be used for drinking water during meals. Article 14: When hiring new workers, preference should be given to new workers recruited within the workshop. Article 15: The grading system in the packing room will be abolished and the old counting system will be used for calculation. Chairman: Gu Bingyuan. Committee Members: Zhou Funong, Zhang Shouchun, Biejishima, Nishimura Nobutomi, Chen Yurong, Chen Aqing. Observers: Li Jinfu. Recorder: Ye Yingtong.

Construction Bureau Solicits Silk Products for Exhibition

The Shanghai County Government recently received an instruction from the Jiangsu Construction Bureau, stating, "Upon receiving an instruction from the Provincial Government, approving a consultation from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, stating that silk is a special product of our country, traditionally used for clothing and a major export. Recently, due to the rapid development of the silk weaving industry in Europe, America, and Japan, the import of foreign products has increased, leading to a decline in various domestic silk industries. The museum, in order to encourage Chinese people to use domestic goods and to thoroughly research silk improvement and weaving, intends to solicit products from silk-producing provinces in the country and hold a domestic silk exhibition at the museum in March and April of this year to encourage and promote learning from each other. The regulations for the domestic silk exhibition and the rules for soliciting products have been drafted and submitted for review. After detailed review by the department, approval has been granted. In addition to the instructions, the relevant regulations and rules from the National Products Exhibition Hall of the Capital regarding the domestic silk exhibition are enclosed and sent to your Provincial Government, requesting you to forward them to the relevant competent authorities and silk industry organizations in your jurisdiction to prepare products for transportation to Beijing for the exhibition. This is hereby copied and sent to the County Magistrate, who shall forward it to the County Chamber of Commerce and silk industry organizations for compliance. This matter concerns the promotion of domestic goods and must not be neglected. This order."

German Committee for Investigating Chinese Tea Arrives in China

▲Mr. Sugen Has Already Departed

▲Expected to Arrive Mid-Next Month

The Berlin Economic Committee of Germany believes that our country produces the most tea and that its quality and taste are superior to teas from other countries. Therefore, it has sent Mr. Sugen to China to investigate tea roasting methods, storage methods, the geology of tea plantations, how fertilizers are used, and the latest statistics on tea production and exports. It is now reported that Mr. Sugen has already departed for China and is expected to arrive in Shanghai in mid-next month. The committee has sent a letter to the Shanghai Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, requesting it to convey to Minister Kong the request to dispatch personnel to guide Mr. Sugen to various tea-producing provinces for investigation upon his arrival in Shanghai. After receiving the letter, the bureau forwarded it to Minister Kong and also sent letters to the governments of Zhejiang and Anhui provinces, requesting them to instruct the relevant authorities in tea-producing areas to provide detailed guidance and protection during his investigation.

Yangsi District Prepares to Establish Cotton Planting Cooperative Experiment Farm

Chen Tianxi, a municipal committee member of the Yangsi District in this city, recognizing the decline of agriculture in the district and the fact that most farmers adhere to old practices without making improvements, resulting in a continuous decline in agricultural income, has donated funds to establish nine cotton planting cooperative experiment farms starting this summer. He has also hired Cheng Bingquan, a technician from the Yangsi cotton experiment farm of the Agricultural College of Central University, as the instructor. Yesterday was the meeting to prepare for the establishment. In addition to various farming households, Qian Zhongnan from the Bureau of Social Affairs also attended to provide guidance. Various specimens were displayed at the meeting, and the instructor, Cheng, gave detailed explanations, which the elderly farmers found quite interesting.

Chamber of Commerce Requests Exemption from National Product Alkaline Powder Tax

The Chamber of Commerce wired the Zhenjiang Office of the Jiangsu Provincial Finance Commissioner of the Ministry of Finance yesterday, stating, "The Yancai Miscellaneous Goods Industry Association believes that the tax office is levying a tax on alkaline powder used by factories. On the 17th of this month, Henry Alkali Factory reported this and telegraphed to your office requesting verification and prohibition. Now, Henry Alkali Factory has sent a letter stating that the Chinese alkaline powder used by the factory is purchased from the Yongli Alkali Manufacturing Company, managed by Jiuda Refined Salt Company, with a formal agreement established. A copy of the shipping document based on the original case approved by the Ministry to exempt the alkaline from levee tax for five years has been attached to the meeting. It is found that Yongli Alkali Manufacturing Company is located in Tanggu, and according to the general method of taxing foreign goods, after paying the export tax at the Tianjin Customs, it can circulate throughout the country, and no more taxes should be levied. Moreover, Yongli alkaline powder has been specially approved for exemption from tax for five years, and the time limit has not yet expired. The tax office is a type of contracted levee collector, and how can it levy a tax on the alkaline powder that has been approved by the Ministry to be exempt, thus disregarding the law and disturbing merchants? According to the previous situation in the letter, a copy of the shipping document is attached and sent to your office requesting verification. Please refer to the previous case and transfer the instructions for compliance with the regulations. Sincerely, the Shanghai Special Municipality Chamber of Commerce Consolidation Committee."
